## intent:cpplus_why_asking
- sao co kieu float roi ma lai co them kieu [double](cpplus_content) chi vay may?
- sao cรณ kiแปu float rแปi mร lแบกi cรณ thรชm kiแปu [double](cpplus_content) chi vแบญy mรy?
- TแบI SAO CแบฆN XรI [ARRAY]{"entity": "cpplus_content", "value": "array"}
- Tai sao lai xai kieu [double](cpplus_content)
- Lรฝ do gรฌ mร lแบกi cรณ [unary operator]{"entity": "cpplus_content", "value": "unary-operator"} thแบฟ?
